    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {

<span id="freeTextContainer4528452432314560629">EDIT AUGUST 31, 2012:<br/>Book comes out at 12:01 EST and I just wanted to say, one more time: THANK YOU ALL FOR THE MOST AMAZING YEAR!<br/><br/>To my Kickstarter contributors who funded me while I wrote this book - I won't forget you and you are immortal in your special edition copies. Thank you so much for respecting my wishes and holding off on your reviews until official release. Thank you for not spoiling this story. And thank you...for being the most amazing fans - ever.<br/><br/>----------------------------------</span>
  <span id="freeText4528452432314560629" style="display:none">EDIT AUGUST 31, 2012:<br />Book comes out at 12:01 EST and I just wanted to say, one more time: THANK YOU ALL FOR THE MOST AMAZING YEAR!<br /><br />To my Kickstarter contributors who funded me while I wrote this book - I won't forget you and you are immortal in your special edition copies. Thank you so much for respecting my wishes and holding off on your reviews until official release. Thank you for not spoiling this story. And thank you...for being the most amazing fans - ever.<br /><br />------------------------------------------------------------------------A note for those of you waiting for the sequel, Seduced in the Dark, BEFORE you read Captive in the Dark: I meant for you to have a break between these two books. I honestly feel that reading them back to back will detract from the experience. The book begins 4 months after the last one and if you haven't had time in between, I think the new tone of the book will throw you off a bit. I don't know for sure, but that's my 'author' input. I didn't split these books up because I wanted to leave you hanging, I did it, so I could leave you breathless.</span>

<div id="review_414258736" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/414258736" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/414258736?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer414258736" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1028463944728815160"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391196i/753387.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391196i/753388.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>5 DARK, EMOTIONALLY MINDFUCKING STARS!!!!!!<br/><br/><b> <i> “Some stories aren’t black and white…” </i> </b> <br/><br/>W.O.W. This series blew me away. I can barely process thought after reading this book.<br/><br/><b> CJ Roberts has written an outstanding novel with a twisted and yet beautiful love story, multi-layered, complex characters that will test the boundaries of your heart and mind, a plot that will captivate and disturb you but at the same time leave you unable to turn away, and a raw, gritty, brutal world of betrayal, revenge, h</b></span>
  <span id="freeText1028463944728815160" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391196i/753387.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391196i/753388.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>5 DARK, EMOTIONALLY MINDFUCKING STARS!!!!!!<br><br><b> <i> “Some stories aren’t black and white…” </i> </b> <br><br>W.O.W. This series blew me away. I can barely process thought after reading this book.<br><br><b> CJ Roberts has written an outstanding novel with a twisted and yet beautiful love story, multi-layered, complex characters that will test the boundaries of your heart and mind, a plot that will captivate and disturb you but at the same time leave you unable to turn away, and a raw, gritty, brutal world of betrayal, revenge, honor, lust, and love. It seduced me and it sickened me. I felt emotionally drained, utterly mindfucked and yet, ultimately, somehow completely at peace. Definitely one of my top favorite reads of the year. </b> <br><br>This book is INTENSE!! It is raw, deeply disturbing and dark, and yet strangely heart warming despite my reading most of it with my heart lodged firmly in my throat. This book stripped my emotions bare. My heart ached to the point of physical pain, and my mind was toyed with to the point where I could barely trust anything I was thinking.<br><br>It is a sweeping, epic, emotional rollercoaster full of unexpected twists and turns. This is a book about the world of sex-trafficking – there are instances of abuse, rape, slavery, BDSM (for real though – no safe word, no consent, no way out). There is no way to sugar-coat that and the author never shies away from telling it exactly how it is. In many ways, I found what happened in this book more disturbing than the first one. Sometimes I would just sit there with my hand over my mouth after scenes going ‘Oh. My. God. Did I really just read that?!” …. and yet at the same time this book opened my heart and mind to things I never thought I could possibly accept.<br><br>This book starts off four months after the end of book 1, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive in the Dark</a>. I won’t say anything about the plot because honestly, anything I say would spoil WAY too much. Suffice it to say, that I LOVED the ending. That alone, should tell you all you need to know about it This book has lots of perspectives and lots of timelines but primarily, we have a dual story line told through a mix of memories that fill in the blanks of events in the past 4 months, as well as a present day story line. And, just like with book 1, we have both Livvie and Caleb’s POVs as well as a new one I’ll let you find out about on your own.<br><br>The story builds. And I mean, it BUILDS. Towards the final 75% I honestly felt like I couldn’t breathe. Couldn’t think. I just sat there with tears in my eyes watching all the pieces of this intricate, horrific, heart wrenching story come together. By the end, I was pretty much just sobbing uncontrollably. It was the perfect ending. My heart felt battered and bruised but I was just so incredibly happy.<br><br>Livvie had grown a lot in this book. I loved her in book 1, but she blew me away in book 2. Her inner strength and the depth of her understanding and compassion was absolutely beautiful. Her uncrushable spirit was what got me through reading some of the darker scenes. She saw Caleb for who he really was. And she knew what she really felt for him. She saw the man behind the monster and was perceptive, forgiving and caring enough to understand why he was the way he was.<br><br><i> <b> “I wanted Caleb. I knew it was stupid. I knew he was a terrible person, who’d done terrible things. I knew he didn’t deserve me or my love. I didn’t care. During the course of our time together, I’d fall in love with my captor. I ‘d fallen in love with his smell and his taste; his smile, kindness, and yes, even his cruelty because I knew it was a part of him.<br>I wanted him to know. I wanted him to know everything and I wanted it to mean something to him. I wanted him to choose me and accept me. I wanted him to leave everything behind and love me.” </b></i>  <br><br>Caleb, Caleb, Caleb… the <i> “monster with a heart of gold” </i> … He is pretty much the epitome of a conflicted, deeply tortured character with possibly one of THE most horrific and heart breaking back stories I’ve ever read. He was cruel, but yet kind; brutal, and yet caring… and his journey was him finding out which side of him was more dominant – the man inside, or the monster he showed the world?<br><br><i> “He had told her he wasn’t her Prince Charming, but what he hasn’t said, was he wished he could be. Once upon a time, he may have been… normal. Before he had been stolen, before the beatings and the rapes and the killing – he could have been something different than what he was.”<br><br>“He didn’t like the feelings running through him…. trying to find the exact moment in which he’d lost control and fallen under the spell of the woman who was supposed to be </i> his <i> captive.” </i> <br><br>There were many, MANY times when I questioned whether or not anything he could ever do could possibly redeem him in my eyes. There were times I hated him, utterly and completely, with every fiber of my being. But then his tenderness would hit my heart so deep, I knew I just couldn’t stop myself from loving him.<br><br>His journey in this book was heart breaking as he struggled between being true to his heart and being true to the intense loyalty he felt for the man that raised him. I got caught up in his struggle – at times I wanted to believe in him and he made me fall in love with his humanity – with the tender, caring, side of him that he couldn't hide from Livvie despite his best efforts, but then the harsh, brutal switch from that to cold hearted trainer would rip my heart out and I’d spiral back into confusion, betrayal and uncertainty.<br><br>Its hard because you find yourself genuinely, honestly, full-heartedly sympathizing with someone involved in human trafficking and murder. But at the same time, you have to consider that he too was violated, for years. It was what he grew up with and the only world he knew. Nothing of what he does is out of outright cruelty. But the tricky part is that that isn’t a justification, but it still makes you question everything you are feeling. Its very thought provoking. Can there ever be redemption for violation? There is no black and white answer.<br><br><i> “Every time I think you’re coming around, every time I let myself hope, you crush me. You rip everything out! Sometimes I think I fucking hate you. Sometimes I know I hate you. And Still! Still, Caleb – I love you. I put my faith in you. I believe you when you say its going to be alright.”<br><br>“Live for me, Kitten. Be all those things you’d never be with me. Go to school. Meet a normal boy and fall in love. Forget me.” </i> *SOB*<br><br>There were times when I’d swoon over how much I wanted them to find a way out of their horrible situation and just end up happily together, and then at other times, the reality of their world, of what was actually happening would just jolt into me and make me sick to my stomach. And yet… against every piece of sane judgement in my mind, I desperately, with all my freaking heart, wanted them to be together.<br><br>CJ Roberts is an absolutely BRILLIANT and phenomenally talented author. Her words just seep into your soul dragging you right into the story. They make you question everything you thought you were sure about and leave hungry for more. The writing style is captivating and enthralling, and the flow of the story is perfect. It opened my mind more than any book I’ve ever read and I know this is one of those stories that has left a mark on my heart and will not be forgotten.<br><br>If you can maintain an open mind, this is one of THOSE amazing series that will stay with you long after you close the pages of the book.<br><br>This is absolutely NOT a stand-alone. YOU MUST READ BOOK 1,<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive in the Dark</a>, FIRST!!!!<br><br>CASTING (See above)<br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1028463944728815160" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer332066788" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12160691448607637674"><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/excited%20gif/NKassirer/Reaction%20Gifs/Happy%20or%20Excited/mabelexcited.gif?o=58' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733571.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b> BEST.FUCKING.BOOK.EVER !!!! </b> <br/><br/>Firstly , before I get on with this review , CJ love this is for you <a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/all%20hail/mrshight/mexicanwave.gif?o=160' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733572.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/clap%20gif/GIFsforhire/Slap-Clap/thankthelord.gif?o=7' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733573.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Oh my dear lord , I am out of words to describe what an amazing book this has turned out to be . Honestly speaking and <i> no offense to reviewers who have reviewed it </i> words cannot comply or even describe or make you realize how good this book is . I mean , no matter what I write here or what you've already read about it can in no way make you experience the intensity of this story . Its </span>
  <span id="freeText12160691448607637674" style="display:none"><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/excited%20gif/NKassirer/Reaction%20Gifs/Happy%20or%20Excited/mabelexcited.gif?o=58" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> BEST.FUCKING.BOOK.EVER !!!! </b> <br><br>Firstly , before I get on with this review , CJ love this is for you <a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/all%20hail/mrshight/mexicanwave.gif?o=160" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/clap%20gif/GIFsforhire/Slap-Clap/thankthelord.gif?o=7" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Oh my dear lord , I am out of words to describe what an amazing book this has turned out to be . Honestly speaking and <i> no offense to reviewers who have reviewed it </i> words cannot comply or even describe or make you realize how good this book is . I mean , no matter what I write here or what you've already read about it can in no way make you experience the intensity of this story . Its up to you pick it up , strap yourself and be lost in what I call a journey of a lifetime . <br><br><b>
  <i> Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.</i>
</b><br><br>Seduced in the Dark was one of my most anticipated reads of the year . With the kind of cliff hanger we were left with in Captive in the Dark , I was dying to find out what was in store for Caleb and Livvie and boy oh boy was I choking with all sorts of emotions when I finished reading it . 2 hours ago , yep , I finished this book 2 hours ago and couldn't bring myself to write a review and express my thoughts on this book . All I could do was stare at my laptop and find the right kinds of words that would do justice to this story . <br><br>Sticking to the idea that most of my friends and reviewers have followed , I will not get into the details of this story . Why ? Because its just impossible to talk about this book and the various feelings that it invokes in you without giving away any spoilers . Like I've mentioned before there is no way a reader is going to understand the evolution , the emotions , the TRUTH of these characters till they've got a taste of it on their own . <br><br>CJ has a unique storytelling technique that keeps you involved in the story and the different scenarios as they keep playing out . I like deducing and predicting the next moves of the story or the characters but with CJ and her uniqueness , there was no way in hell that I could guess anything correctly . One minute I found myself smiling and the next I was trying to control the tears that were prickling on the edges of my eyes . I agree , I cried . There was no way I couldn't . It made me think of the twisted world we live in , where humanity has lost its meaning . In a world where power and money are the only language spoken . I also realized Love has many forms and different colors . And that it means different things to different people . Some of it may not seem right to us , but it may be the only thing for those who see it that way . <br><br>Caleb's past had me reeling and I wanted to hug him and tell him things would be okay . As for Livvie , that girl never ceases to amaze me . She was just amazing . Even after everything that she was going through her love for Caleb stood strong . There were times I wanted to throttle Caleb for treating her wrong , but I couldn't bring myself to hate him ... Oh god , I'm border lining 'spoilers'ville here so I better shut up . <br><br> <br>Seduced in the Dark , a heart wrenching , compelling , erotically beautiful and seducing read will leave you marked forever and Caleb and Livvie's journey will remain in the hearts of the readers for years to come . <br><br>5 stars is just soooo not happening for this book . Infinite stars to this one from , its definitely a MUST READ !<br><br>CJ Roberts , for such an amazing story : <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/thank%20you%20gif/javaflip/Thank_you.gif?o=9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380378132ra/733574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>

<div id="review_432767660" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/432767660" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/432767660?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=favorite-series">favorite-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer432767660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6592143497897070465"><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390542i/752283._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>And the story of Caleb and Livvie continues...</i>
</b><br/><br/>Again, it's a very <b>intense, dark, powerful and highly captivating</b> story that constantly kept me on the edge of my seat while reading it. To be honest, this book probably wasn't that good for my mental health...the last few chapters got me so worked up and I was so anxious to finish it that I nearly felt like crying if I didn't find out soon how the stor</span>
  <span id="freeText6592143497897070465" style="display:none"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390542i/752283._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>And the story of Caleb and Livvie continues...</i>
</b><br><br>Again, it's a very <b>intense, dark, powerful and highly captivating</b> story that constantly kept me on the edge of my seat while reading it. To be honest, this book probably wasn't that good for my mental health...the last few chapters got me so worked up and I was so anxious to finish it that I nearly felt like crying if I didn't find out soon how the story ended... but after all, I was soooo happy I stuck through with it because <i>Seduced in the Dark</i> truly is one of the best books I've ever read...<br><br><br><blockquote>
<b><u>WARNING:</u></b> this review might contain spoilers for those who haven't read part one of the Dark Duet series yet...</blockquote><br><br><br><b>
  <u>The Story</u>
</b><br><br>At the end of <i>Captive in the Dark</i> we learn that Caleb has informed Livvie of his plan to train her and sell her as a pleasure slave to his biggest enemy Demitri Balk (aka Vladek Rostrovich). But we also found out that Caleb and Livvie are starting to have feelings for each other...feelings that they can't simply seem to ignore. The question now is, what will prevail to Caleb? His lifelong quest for revenge and his debt to Rafiq, the man who once saved his life or his newfound happiness in being with Livvie, the girl that has made him see there might be more to life than the sole purpose of revenge...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"He had told her he wasn't her Prince Charming, but what he hadn't said, was he wished he could be."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>To tell you much more about the story would be spoiling to much. Therefore I would advice you to just experience it for yourself... Just like in the first part of the series, there are some very twisted, mind-boggling scenes in <i>Seduced in the Dark</i> but in the end, it all makes perfect sense as to why everything happened the way it did...<br><br><br><u>
  <b>Caleb</b>
</u><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394093i/758759.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>A tortured soul...<br><br>A monster with a heart of gold...<br><br>Monsters aren't born the way they are, they are made into it by the circumstances they're given...</i>
</b><br><br><i>Caleb, Caleb, Caleb...</i> One moment I hated him, the next I loved him, after that I hated him again, then he did something that me love him again... Seems very messed up, I know... But that was exactly the kind of character he was. Twisted, dark and constantly changing his mind. It was hard, trying to understand why he handled things the way he did... At times he really infuriated the hell out of me; for example <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[when he wanted to punish Livvie for leading him on by simply making her stand by and watch while he was having sex with Celia <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I've been doing this a long time - manipulating people to get my way. That's why you think you love me. Because I've broken you down and built you back up to believe it. It wasn't an accident. Once you leave this behind...you'll see that."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Caleb himself thinks he's a monster, incapable of loving or receiving love from anyone. But slowly he begins to realize that maybe underneath it all, he's still a person capable of having the exact same feelings everyone else has. And Livvie is the one who finally makes him see the world he's been living in, in a different perspective.<br><br><u>
  <b>Livvie</b>
</u><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394093i/758760.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"My name is Kitten and my master is gone. What could possibly be more important?"</b><br><br>Livvie has really changed over the past few months... After being held captive for so long and after going through so many horrible events <i>"the naïve girl in her had been bitch-slapped into womanhood"</i>. When we first meet her in <i>Seduced in the Dark</i>, Caleb and Livvie have been separated from each other and Livvie is being held under custody by the FBI. There, Agent Reed and Dr. Sloan (two new interesting side characters) are trying to put the pieces back to together of what happened to Livvie while was being held by Caleb.<br><br>Agent Reed and Dr. Sloan are constantly questioning her about every little detail she remembers from her time with Caleb and for that she has to live through all her memories. Memories of Caleb that remind her of the fact she may never see him again... Since the first time we've gotten to know Livvie, she has also gotten a much more snarky attitude and I really loved that about her.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"For the love of Christ, shut - up! Let a bitch enjoy her mental breakdown in peace."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Livvie has been through so much, she's been broken down into a million pieces, but still she manages to stay strong through it all... Just like in <i>Captive in the Dark</i> I highly admired her strength and her power to resist and stand up for herself in so many ways. I found myself constantly hoping she would finally get the happy ending she was so desperately hoping for... <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I love you, Caleb. I love you! If you care for me at all...please, don't do this! Please don't leave me. I don't know how to live without you. Don't make me go back to trying to be someone I don't know how to be anymore."<br><br>** <br><br>"Live for me, Kitten. Be all those things you'd never be with me. Go to school. Meet a normal boy and fall in love. Forget me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><br>The author, <b>CJ Roberts</b>, has really done a magnificent job at creating this unique and powerful series with a very thought provoking content. She makes you go through all the emotions Caleb and Livvie go through and I really became a fan of her captivating writing style. I already know I'm looking forward to reading much more of her work in the future!!!!<br><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394093ra/758761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It was ironic, because at first, I hated the dark. I had spent so much time those first few weeks of my captivity, craving the sun and the light on my face. Suddenly, it seemed the opposite. In the dark, my master let down his guard and he was Caleb again. He didn't correct me. He didn't punish me. He didn't push me away emotionally. Caleb was there to hold me until the nightmares passed. He was there to tell me I was beautiful. He was there to tell me I was going to be okay. In the dark, he seduced me. I didn't want the seduction to end."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380394093i/758762.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><br><br>*****<br><br><br>To everyone who hasn't read the Dark Duet series yet, I would say: <u>give it a try</u>!!!<br><br><br>You might feel like the story is getting too much and you might want to stop reading it altogether, but thrust me: It'll be worth it...<br><br><br>And to truly understand why everyone keeps raving about this book so much, you have to read it till the very last page...<br><br><br><br>ENJOY!!!</b><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="6592143497897070465" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_335182778" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/335182778" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/335182778?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=bdsm-kink">bdsm-kink</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=gamma-hero">gamma-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=human-trafficking-slavery">human-trafficking-slavery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tortured-abused-hero">tortured-abused-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-erotica">dark-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=mind-f-ckery">mind-f-ckery</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer335182778" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2739430593336302545"><i>‘If it be thus to dream, still let me sleep’ – William Shakespeare</i><br/><br/>At long last, the much anticipated second instalment of the Dark Duet and if you thought Captive in the Dark took your breath away, then Seduced in the Dark will stop your heart.<br/><br/>It’s such an incredible story with so many unexpected, unforeseen twists that even up until the last few pages, I couldn’t see how it would end. There’s such great depth to the story that you just don’t find very often in a lot of sex-slavery style novels </span>
  <span id="freeText2739430593336302545" style="display:none"><i>‘If it be thus to dream, still let me sleep’ – William Shakespeare</i><br /><br />At long last, the much anticipated second instalment of the Dark Duet and if you thought Captive in the Dark took your breath away, then Seduced in the Dark will stop your heart.<br /><br />It’s such an incredible story with so many unexpected, unforeseen twists that even up until the last few pages, I couldn’t see how it would end. There’s such great depth to the story that you just don’t find very often in a lot of sex-slavery style novels – it’s intricately woven and shocking and stopped me in my tracks. Everything got dropped – the need to finish this novel, to find out how it could possibly end was just all consuming.<br /><br />I’d read CJ Roberts saying somewhere that these 2 books were designed to be read with a break in between so, with that in mind, I didn’t reread Captive and went straight into this one. The story is told in 2 different timelines and alternating POV’s. It’s a little confusing to begin with but the story is so dynamic, you’re soon sucked in and it may start out slowly but it gathers pace like a runaway train.<br /><br />We start with Olivia incarcerated in the present in a mental institution being interrogated by the FBI, by an agent with his own dark sexual proclivities, sometime after the events of the book and also the story is told in retrospect as we pick up Olivia and Caleb where we left them at the end of Captive.<br /><br />At the start of this book, Olivia is a lifetime away from the person she was at the beginning of Captive – she’s been bitchslapped into womanhood by her experiences. Caleb, despite his feelings for Olivia, is still consumed by his burning desire for revenge. He’s extremely conflicted, giving Olivia constantly mixed messages – sometimes he is just her Master but, in the dark, he is Caleb and he cares deeply for her. Caleb is a man who has been razed by pain, grief and suffering and honed into what he is by lust, rage and the need to survive. He may be a monster but monsters are made not born and he is the sum total of his lifetime of awful experiences but does the cruelty done to him justify the cruelty he deals out? <br /><br />Despite her injuries, Caleb continues with Olivia’s sex-slave training but he’s inconsistent despite his burning need for vengeance and he’s also training Olivia to pick and choose her battles – to accept the ones she can’t win and to fight the ones she can. She has grown up so fast, has a backbone of steel and an undeniable spirit and she knows she loves Caleb with her heart of hearts – she doesn’t believe for a second that Caleb has broken her down and built her back up to believe she loves him. Caleb denies this – for a long time, vengeance seems to be the only thing he can understand and he tries to convince Olivia that she doesn’t really love him.<br /><br />To go further into this would just spoil the plot and it’s such an amazing story, you just have to experience it and run the gamut of emotions for yourself. It’s such a rush of anguish, despair, hope and love. Of course, as this is a sex-slavery story, there’s scenes of abuse and non-consensual sexual acts so be aware of this before you embark on this and this book absolutely does not stand alone. You MUST read Captive in the Dark first.<br /><br />This is going to be a very hard act to follow both for me as a reader and for CJ Roberts as an author and I feel a book hangover coming on already but I do look forward to whatever her deviant, twisted, brilliant mind can come up with next.<br /><br />5 stars exemplary dark erotica<br /><br />For more of my reviews, please visit my <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Blog</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="2739430593336302545" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=dark">dark</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer437580410" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16680828547999273740"><i>
  <b>He told her he wasn't her prince charming, but what he hadn't said, was he wished he could be...</b>
</i><br/><br/>Many readers struggle to decide whether or not this series is one they'd recommend due to its explicit, no-holds-barred topics and darkly disturbing scenarios--and rightfully so. Upon completion of this emotionally conflicting series, I can safely say that I in fact WOULD recommend these books; although not without fair warning. <br/><br/>As you have probably already discovered, these books are not easy rea</span>
  <span id="freeText16680828547999273740" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>He told her he wasn't her prince charming, but what he hadn't said, was he wished he could be...</b>
</i><br><br>Many readers struggle to decide whether or not this series is one they'd recommend due to its explicit, no-holds-barred topics and darkly disturbing scenarios--and rightfully so. Upon completion of this emotionally conflicting series, I can safely say that I in fact WOULD recommend these books; although not without fair warning. <br><br>As you have probably already discovered, these books are not easy reads. <i>Captive in The Dark</i> took every notion I've held regarding 'dark literature' and rendered them naive. I became emotionally defeated and undone. <i>Seduced in The Dark</i> took this emotions miles further...<br><br>Seduced kicks off with a heartbreaking visual of Livvie in her declining and destructive mental state. She has been captured yet again, this time by the law. The story begins in present time, and it methodically flows in and out of horrific flashbacks that command the majority of this story. <br><br>Never before have I been so emotionally conflicted while reading a book. The author presents a hundred and one legit reasons to hate Caleb, and then, while you're least expecting it, sneaks in surprising shimmers of Caleb's 'human' side causing you to question your stance entirely. You can actually FEEL Caleb's internal frustration as he struggles to push away the unfamiliar feelings of love creeping in; willing himself to focus on his original plan of revenge.<br><br> At first, it felt wrong rooting for the twisted, demented underdog. But as I slowly began to realize that Caleb was not <b>evil</b> trying to overcome, but<b> goodness</b>—wrapped securely within a self-preserving blanket of misery, which he fought hard to maintain—I was able to see him in a whole new light. <br><br>As far as torment is concerned, Livvie faces more brutal, degrading encounters within this installment...as does Caleb. We are presented with details of Caleb's past and it is actually more heartbreaking than I could have imagined. I vowed to never love Caleb. But in the end, with my emotions running rapid, I can honestly say that my dutiful vow had long been forgotten. <br><br>The Dark Duet has given me a solid pair of reading wings; I truly feel freer and more courageous in stepping outside of my comfort zone without feeling overwhelmed...and I have this series to thank for that!<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Dark Erotica<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum/disturbing <br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Unconventional, but slowly evolves. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Greater, in-depth perception into the heart of their pain.<br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Continues. Deals with the residual tragedy, and offers numerous, heartbreaking flashbacks.<br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Raw, fearless, and profound.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine.<br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> An epilogue from Caleb's perspective. <br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_358700938" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/358700938" />
    <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club"><img alt="Stacia (the 2010 club)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417661051p2/4013351.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/358700938?book_show_action=true">Jun 30, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stacia (the 2010 club)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stacia (the 2010 club)" href="/user/show/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club">Stacia (the 2010 club)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who can handle dark and disturbing books</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=bdsm-or-person-in-control">bdsm-or-person-in-control</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=romantica-or-erotica">romantica-or-erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=dark-or-taboo">dark-or-taboo</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4013351-stacia-the-2010-club?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer358700938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10557131828392213100"><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"Kitten," he said, "monsters can't love."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/>By the time I reached the halfway point of this book, I was ready to slap a big fat 1 star rating on this review and write a vengeful spiel. <b>Yes, that's right. 1 star. I was seeing red. I was RAGING with fury.</b><br/><br/>So, you ask, "why now the 4 star rating?" Well, let's see...<br/><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>It felt wrong to fantasize about such things - but Caleb didn't care. Fantasies were all he could have and no one could take them from him.</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/>This book would have been c</span>
  <span id="freeText10557131828392213100" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"Kitten," he said, "monsters can't love."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>By the time I reached the halfway point of this book, I was ready to slap a big fat 1 star rating on this review and write a vengeful spiel. <b>Yes, that's right. 1 star. I was seeing red. I was RAGING with fury.</b><br><br>So, you ask, "why now the 4 star rating?" Well, let's see...<br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>It felt wrong to fantasize about such things - but Caleb didn't care. Fantasies were all he could have and no one could take them from him.</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>This book would have been complete shit without Caleb's point of view. If we had only seen Caleb through Livvie's eyes, we would have never fully understood him.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>Caleb could feel Livvie's tears as they slid down her face. It was as close to crying as Caleb could get and for a moment he imagined they were his tears. They were his confessions. They said all the things he couldn't...because he was a coward.</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The only way this book was going to work meant that Caleb's bad side had to continue to show on the outside while he was struggling internally with the idea of how to let down his guard. If he had gone soft too soon, or if he had gone completely soft, every single part of this book would have become a farce. I am thankful that neither of the former things happened. Caleb was <i>never</i> romanticized. This is a crucial element of a taboo read. The second the story becomes romanticized, the credibility is gone. We as the reader can feel emotion, sympathy, even fondness for these characters, but we need to be kept in the cold, hard truth that THIS situation is NOT good. That THESE people are SCREWED up. As long as we continue to see things for what they are, then we can allow ourselves to be swept away in the lives and emotions of our characters. <br><br>This story was just as much of a thrill ride as it was a mind screw. I was <b>entertained.</b> I was <b>angered.</b> I was <b>scared.</b> I was <b>hesitant.</b> I even found some <b>grain of contentment</b> when it was all said and done. <br><br>Yes, there was a scene before the halfway point which had me angrier at any book scene (and I can easily recall at least 3 books which have had a similar sort of betrayal scene that did not anger me even half as much as this one did) than I'd ever been. So much so, that I was <i>this close</i> to quitting out on the read. Even now, I'm still pissy when I think about what went down.<br><br>But at least I got some satisfaction in this:<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"I guess you do want revenge," Ruthless me whispered.<br><u>You bet your sweet ass, I do.</u></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm grateful that this author was able to turn things around for me. I didn't have much faith, to be honest. In the end, the story was quite the entertaining journey. The <u>Dark Duet</u> may not be an easy read, but it's definitely an interesting one. I hope to read more from C.J. Roberts in the future.<br><br>Not to be too much of a fly in the ointment but...<br><br><b>There were a few minor complaints :</b><br><br>1. This book needed more editing. Aside from the obvious swapping of <i>you're</i> and <i>your</i>, as well as a few typos, there were several instances where sentences probably should have been rearranged for easier readability. Given that I'm a huge comma abuser (I stick them everywhere in a haphazard fashion), I won't try to argue where the commas should go, but even I had a few moments of wondering if there was a better way to get a point across other than slapping in a bunch of commas to break up sentences :<br><br><i>"So, according to Caleb and Muhammad Rafiq, Demitri Balk, also referred to as, Vladek Rostrovich, is supposed to be there?</i><br><br><blockquote>or another example...</blockquote><br><i>"Will, Rafiq, be there?"</i><br><br>2. There were too many "styles" of writing going on : There were past scenes and there were present scenes - sometimes switching when you didn't know it was going to happen. The first couple of chapters took some getting used to. Aside from the regular past and present scenes, there were also memories, dreams and flashbacks in italics. As well, there were also first person points of view mixed with third person points of view. If just a couple of methods had been used instead of all of the above, the read would have felt more cohesive than it did.<br><br><b>End note...</b> This part's my fault. Even though I warn against romanticizing this story, I can't help but imagine Paul Walker as Caleb ever since someone else brought him up as a casting choice. And hot damn, it's a strange war in my head not to drool over the rapist, slave-holding asshole when he's this hot. Apparently, I'm warped...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379775815i/347769.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="10557131828392213100" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="xrysa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="xrysa" href="/user/show/9016476-xrysa">xrysa</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer419700052" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17033847856507589113"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389927i/751308._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>“I've been doing this a long time- manipulating people to get my way. That's why you think you love me. Because I've broken you down and built you back up to believe it. It wasn't an accident. Once you leave this behind..... you'll see that. -Caleb”</b><br/><br/><i>After all these is it possible for her to move on?</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392034i/754837.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Is he a monster?</i><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754838.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>“Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.”</i><br/><b>Olivia</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390542i/752277._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>“She kisses my scars and I create new ones for her.”</i><br/><b>Caleb</b><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>In this book Livvie has ma</span>
  <span id="freeText17033847856507589113" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389927i/751308._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“I've been doing this a long time- manipulating people to get my way. That's why you think you love me. Because I've broken you down and built you back up to believe it. It wasn't an accident. Once you leave this behind..... you'll see that. -Caleb”</b><br><br><i>After all these is it possible for her to move on?</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392034i/754837.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Is he a monster?</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754838.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.”</i><br><b>Olivia</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380390542i/752277._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“She kisses my scars and I create new ones for her.”</i><br><b>Caleb</b><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>In this book Livvie has managed to escape from Caleb and she is safe at a hospital.She has to tell Reed what happened , in order to find the auction and stop these awful people . She also has to tell Dr Sloan ,so she can help her recover and the story starts.<br><br><i>Then</i><br>Caleb took her at Felipe's estate and there he showed Rafiq their slave's progress . Rafiq was not satisfied with Livvie but Caleb tried to reassure him that she would be improved .<br>From the moment that he saved her from the bikers Caleb was treating her more gently than he should and they came closer to each other.<br><br>I was relieved that Caleb didnt hurt her anymore but the book started becoming darker at Felipe's party.<br>Felipe's slave , Celia , entertained them a lot by torturing Kid.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754839.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754840.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb's emotions were changing all the time.<br>During the day he liked to be called <i>Master</i>, he liked to treat her like a slave but only when the others were around.<br>During the night he was comforting and kind .<br><br>This whole situation led them to develop what they had.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754841.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Mine.<br>Mine.<br>Mine.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754842.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And then that bastard ,Felipe , ruined everything.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754843.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Caleb was being manipulated so he did things that frustrated me a lot.<br><br><b>“Dealing with Caleb was all about perspective. You couldn’t appreciate his kindness until you’d felt his cruelty.”</b><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[1)The celar scene <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754844.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[2)When he hit her <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754845.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[3)The diner where he humiliated the hell out of her <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380332181ra/692856.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However Livvie didnt give up on him.Her plan to seduce him worked but she fell for him as well.Caleb admited only that he cared for her because monsters cant love.<br><br>They would sell her but Felipe (thanks god!) talked to Caleb about his past and what really happened to him.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392034ra/754846.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I couldnt believe what I was reading.<br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Everything was a lie.Omg I wanted to kill Rafiq but thankfully Caleb did it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><i>Present</i><br>Livvie is free now but she cant forget what happened to her but mostly Caleb.He is haunting her thoughts and that's driving her crazy.<br>She needs help because according to everyone that isnt healthy.<br>She is still in love with Caleb but that's not happening because she is suffering from Stockholm sydrom.<br>Caleb was the only one who cared about her in his unique and twisted way.Livvie grew up without love and yet she managed to be loved by him.<br><br><u>Livvie</u>:I really admire her.Maybe she is crying all the time but try to put yourself in her shoes.What she'd been through wasnt easy.The way that he loved her wasnt fair.Despite all the difficulties she managed to stay on her feet and move on.<br><br><u>Caleb</u>:He is not prince charming , he never was but he wished he could be for her.He wished he could be her hero.He saved her life once but he keeps putting her in danger again and he hates himself for doing it.According to him monsters cant love and Livvie gave him a present he didnt deserve.<br><br><b>“Tell me you love me, Caleb," I whispered.<br>He kissed me, refusing. "I wish I could, Kitten”</b><br><br><br>I never thought that I would like a book character like Caleb.He is awful and sometimes I wanted to kill him but he was fucked up. Still that doesnt justify his awful actions but reading the epilogue I understood many things about him.<br><br><br><br><u>The last chapter and the epilogue</u>.<br>I never thought that I would cry so much with this book.I was a sobbing mess and hate it when it's happening.<br><br>All started when Caleb said:<br><b>"I love you Livvie."<br>He put the key in the ignitation and drove away.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380344239ra/699286.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“Live for me, Kitten. Be all those things you'd never be with me. Go to school. Meet a normal boy and fall in love. Forgive me. It's time for you to go, Kitten. Time for us both, to go.”</b><br><br>And then I think that I read the most beautiful epilogue all time.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380372203ra/725446.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Many people are judging this book and I totally understand them.<br>On the other hand I love this book because it delievers with its own way a few messages.<br>All of us should be gratefull that we have our freedom and no matter what happens we should stay strong and never break.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311518ra/688494.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <span id="freeText13738950906760429173" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391318ra/753589.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>I was totally blown away by Seduced in the Dark!!<br>It's a dark read and I felt irritation,disgust and shock..<br>But in the same time it hooked me completely!It was intense in a total mind fuck!!It was disturbing and hot to the same time..<br>I never thought I would like it,but I loved it!It makes me feel things I had never felt!!<br><br><br>Caleb and Livvie's journey was one of the most painful things I've ever read..Their story is beyond disturbing,scary and sad..<br><br><br><b>“In the dark, he seduced me.I didn't want the seduction to end.”</b><br><br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391318i/753590.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Livvie is safe and she's in the custody of the FBI.Livvie begins to tell Agent Reed and Dr.Sloan her story...<br>We go back and forth between the time period and the present time with Livvie at the FBI and then way in the past when Caleb was young.This  genius way of telling the story will keep you completely hooked!!<br><br><br>Livie was brave,witty,strong,patient,fighter,loyal and most of all she truly was a survivor!! <br><br><br>OMG!!Caleb...I fell in love for the boy he once was..My heart broke when I read his story and I hated the man he became while trying to be what Rafic expected of him...There are times when you will absolutely hate him and wonder why Olivia would even fall in love with him.But then in the end for me he is worthy of her love...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391318ra/753591.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>What I enjoyed most about this book was reading about Caleb and Livvie falling in love.The sweet moments he would let her call him by his name and he would call her Livvie and not Pet.They were so tender and real, giving the book such emotion..<br>Loved every emotion this book gave me <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380391318i/753592._SY540_.jpg" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“Kiss me,” she whispered. It was an offer of distraction.He took it."</b><br><b>"Please Caleb!"I sobbed loudly."Don't do this.Take me and let's go.Let's leave."</b><br><b>"There.Now you're part of me forever.You're mine Livie.I hope you understand." </b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391318ra/753593.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I was wondering how is this all going to end??</b><br><br>This is the most important thing about this book!!<br>It gives you a happy ending and you remember happy things about it at the end...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380391318ra/753594.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br> <br> </span>

    <a title="Yeasmin Alo (Red Sparrow)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/87533127-yeasmin-alo-red-sparrow"><img alt="Yeasmin Alo (Red Sparrow)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604153742p2/87533127.jpg" /></a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87533127-yeasmin-alo-red-sparrow?shelf=painfully-good-dare-not-to-reread">painfully-good-dare-not-to-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/87533127-yeasmin-alo-red-sparrow?shelf=5-fly-me-to-the-moon-stars">5-fly-me-to-the-moon-stars</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3536107451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11732897882416192199"><b>Isn't it shameful that a bad person can create so many MONSTERS just by his deeds?</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599588563i/30079387._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow this book is my biggest Taboo read so far and it was unpleasantly close to my boundaries. <br/><br/>So do I recommend this book?<br/>-NO!<br/><br/>If previous book's brutality was 10 then it is 100<br/><br/><b>But if you actually consciously take the decision to read the book then Pls DON’T DNF it,that will create a massive misunderstanding and misjudgment in your head</b><br/><br/>The book is so well written<br/>It again felt like I am Olivia or I am sitting right b</span>
  <span id="freeText11732897882416192199" style="display:none"><b>Isn't it shameful that a bad person can create so many MONSTERS just by his deeds?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599588563i/30079387._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow this book is my biggest Taboo read so far and it was unpleasantly close to my boundaries. <br><br>So do I recommend this book?<br>-NO!<br><br>If previous book's brutality was 10 then it is 100<br><br><b>But if you actually consciously take the decision to read the book then Pls DON’T DNF it,that will create a massive misunderstanding and misjudgment in your head</b><br><br>The book is so well written<br>It again felt like I am Olivia or I am sitting right beside her listening to her story.<br><br>You will get three POVS<br>√Livvie<br>√Caleb (as usual Narrated in thrid person)<br>√Agent Reed aka Matthew (I am super glad for Reed's perspective it was much needed)<br><br>And Yes Finally I am calling it<br><b>Dark Romance</b><br><br>I'll tell you why-<br><br>1.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <b>Cheating:</b> My heart literally bleed there. Cheating is my biggest trigger <br>I just can't...... <br>Though it depends on the circumstances like in the first book it didn’t matter but in the second book oh my god I just felt pure agony <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>2.Now I am understanding how romanticized, Fantasized Fifty shades of Grey has made BDSM.<br>The real thing is actually cruel and brutal.<br>Also now I've a clear idea why Christian used to call himself Sadist because it is nothing but Sadistic. <br>It was a pure Neon sign and Red flag for me. It'll haunt me for a while.<br><br>3. Caleb, that b***h has multiple personality disorder 😑 as I said in my previous review. He needs medication and spending two books with him now I also feel like I need medication 😂 He is a pure manipulator. <br><br>4.Again I felt so pained that he is not a random Caleb. Why he has to be the abnormal, the lifeless Master Caleb. You will be hating him and you will be loving him<br>Caleb will make you question YOUR morals. <br>It’s utterly frustrating situation.<br><br>5. With Caleb you will always be on square one. You wouldn’t be progressing or deflating.You will be still.<br>He is the savior, he is the villain. He is everything. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599588563i/30079388.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>6.Chapter 18 and 19 I couldn’t take it. I was hard to digest that much I can say.<br><br>7.Untill the first half of the book it was between 3 to 3.5 for me. I was so annoyed and angry that why the author is romanticizing that sadistic sociopath . <br>But HOLD your horses there is a lot to tell beyond your imagination 🤐 Mr. James Bond 2.0<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1599588563i/30079389._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am kinda feeling philosophical<br>So don't mind me but here is my philosophy 😂<br>⬇️⬇️⬇️<br><br><i>Hero imprints on you<br>But Villain leaves scratch on your soul</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_954132866" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/954132866" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/954132866?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=give-me-that-alpha-male">give-me-that-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=panty-soaking-wet">panty-soaking-wet</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=swoon-worthy-guys">swoon-worthy-guys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=im-gonna-need-therapy">im-gonna-need-therapy</a>,
