          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer954132866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8453311182853535242"><b>5 KITTEN STARS ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418056963i/12651536.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“He was there to tell me I was beautiful. He was there to tell me I was going to be okay. In the dark, he seduced me. I didn’t want the seduction to end.”</i>
</b> <br/><br/><b>WOW.</b> This book just catapulted the series from a 3.5 stars to a 5 stars one for me. So to say that I am completely blown away by this read is mildly putting it. Honestly after seeing all the buzz on this series and not entirely loving the first one, I thought I was going to be in the minority but <i>damn</i>. I love being prov</span>
  <span id="freeText8453311182853535242" style="display:none"><b>5 KITTEN STARS ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418056963i/12651536.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“He was there to tell me I was beautiful. He was there to tell me I was going to be okay. In the dark, he seduced me. I didn’t want the seduction to end.”</i>
</b> <br><br><b>WOW.</b> This book just catapulted the series from a 3.5 stars to a 5 stars one for me. So to say that I am completely blown away by this read is mildly putting it. Honestly after seeing all the buzz on this series and not entirely loving the first one, I thought I was going to be in the minority but <i>damn</i>. I love being proved wrong.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380418013ra/827377.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first book definitely laid down the right amount of groundwork for Caleb &amp; Livvie aka 'Kitten', setting the tone of the series and later propelled <b>
  <u>Seduced in the Dark</u>
</b> onto a whole new level of darkness. CJ Roberts spun such a profoundly emotional read that <b>holds back no barriers</b> when dealing with such a disturbing topic that would leave her readers appalled yet compelled by it. <br><br><b>Disturbing, intense and gritty</b>; I devoured this book up in no time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397353i/766600.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“The naïve girl in me had been bitch-slapped into womanhood. I’d been razed by pain, grief, loss and suffering, and honed by lust, rage and an acute awareness of my need to survive.”</i>
</blockquote> <br>One thing that made this book an absolute winner for me is <b>how the characterization on Caleb and Livvie was amazingly done.</b> This book left me feeling strongly for both MCs equally as you witnessed the transformation. <b>Caleb</b>; the amount of love and hatred for him that I struggled internally with but ultimately capturing my heart. <b>Livvie</b>; her resilience, her strong belief and <i>her love for her captor</i>, my heart and mind was at war just as Livvie was when it comes to loving Caleb. <br><br>Put them both together, you'll feel the turmoil of emotions they put you through because in the most unimaginable ways, <b>they found love in the darkness.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.”</i>
</blockquote> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418061770ra/12652967.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>CJ Roberts' method of <b>storytelling was flawless and flowed effortlessly</b> with the way she weaved in the present time with flashbacks of events leading up to the present. <b>The more it unfolds, the more the story intensifies.</b> It's the kind of read that captivates you from the start, grips you throughout and leaves you overwhelmed by the end of it. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>““I've been doing this a long time- manipulating people to get my way. That's why you think you love me. Because I've broken you down and built you back up to believe it. It wasn't an accident. Once you leave this behind...you'll see that.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415443863i/11789676.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I've read a good amount of dark reads and to be amazed and left stumped by one like this, it really does take some mad skills (and a whole lot of messed-up stuff that give me the cringes &amp; shudders). After being spoilt by authors like Lily White and Pepper Winters to deliver me the dark gems, I'm going to need add CJ Roberts to that list. <br><br>This is a read that many will find it hard to stomach, leave you shaken to its core but you'll walk out of it feeling like you've just witnessed something epic and lastly, a sense of loss to see it end. <br><br><b>It was brilliant, it was helluva dark and it was pretty darn phenomenal if I must say.</b> This is an <u>ABSOLUTE must-read</u> by all dark romance junkies and why has it taken me over a year to read it? I frankly don't know; just like I don't have the answer to life but I'm gonna have to kick myself for that.<br><br><i>♥ Buddy Read with Sandy &amp; Kirsten! ♥</i><br><br><i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13612739.Seduced_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___2_" title="Seduced in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #2) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Seduced in the Dark</a> is the second part of the Dark Duet series and cannot be read as a standalone.</i> </span>
  <a data-text-id="8453311182853535242" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer447829073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8321759755356839047"><b>
  <i>Dealing with Caleb was all about perspective. You couldn’t appreciate his kindness until you’d felt his cruelty.</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416168135i/11906396._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='600' alt='belt' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>What a Wicked Erotic Feast!! Holy Hell, I am a sick fuck!! How can my heart belong to murdering, human trafficking, rapist!?!? And not only did I fall for him, I wanted him to have a HEA befitting a true hero. But Caleb is no prince charming. He is the monster that nightmares are made of.<br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Caleb</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415676578i/11828216._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='170' alt='caleb' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Olivia has been through hell. She's been beaten, abducted, raped, and told that she wi</span>
  <span id="freeText8321759755356839047" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Dealing with Caleb was all about perspective. You couldn’t appreciate his kindness until you’d felt his cruelty.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416168135i/11906396._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="belt" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>What a Wicked Erotic Feast!! Holy Hell, I am a sick fuck!! How can my heart belong to murdering, human trafficking, rapist!?!? And not only did I fall for him, I wanted him to have a HEA befitting a true hero. But Caleb is no prince charming. He is the monster that nightmares are made of.<br><br><br><b>
  <i>Caleb</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415676578i/11828216._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="170" alt="caleb" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Olivia has been through hell. She's been beaten, abducted, raped, and told that she will become a sex slave. Livvie is a survivor that has managed to stay strong. But even she is afraid that all of Caleb's mind fuckery has affected her. Because, how can a sane person love their captor?<br><br><br><b>
  <i>During the course of our time together, I’d fallen in love with my captor. I’d fallen in love with his smell and his taste; his smile, kindness, and yes, even his cruelty because I knew it was a part of him.</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416123739i/11894929.jpg" width="400" height="290" alt="kneel" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>Caleb has wanted Livvie from the moment he laid eyes on her. But she was never meant to be his. She was just a tool. A weapon to be used for revenge. <br><br><br><b>
  <i>He didn’t like the feelings running through him. He replayed the incident in his mind, trying to find the exact moment in which he’d lost control and fallen under the spell of the woman who was supposed to be his captive. </i>
</b><br><br><br>Damn these two were beyond intense! Their passion was off the charts. Caleb's jealousy over his Kitten was palpable and almost violent. Livvie was a pawn to be used sexually, but Caleb couldn't stand the thought of another man touching her.<br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415676578i/11828217._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="267" alt="bed" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>“I don’t want revenge, Caleb. I don’t want to end up like you, letting some fucking vendetta run my life. I just want my freedom. I want to be free, Caleb. Not someone’s whore…not even yours.”</i>
</b><br><br><br>Be prepared for an emotional roller coaster. You will experience a vast range of emotions while reading this book. Sympathy, Hope, Disgust, Lust, Hate, Love, Despair, and Doubt. <br><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1415436705i/11788374.jpg" width="400" height="266" alt="bloddy" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This book had it all. It was a Wicked Erotic feast! Fast paced but very thorough. CJ Roberts weaves a violent tale of lust, love, trust, and the ultimate betrayal. There is blackmail, murder, rape, and violence.There were jaw dropping moments that I would have never predicted. The secondary characters are so vivid and have depth. I loved Felipe and Celia's characters. And Agents Sloan and Reed were perfect. I craved more of them also<br><br>There is no black or white. The lines get blurred and everything is gray. You will hate a character one moment, then feel sympathy or love for them two chapters later. I have to admire any author that can play my emotions with such ease. I look forward to more from C.J. Roberts because she really brought her A game with this series!!<br><br></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=books-i-own">books-i-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3078175-rhonda?shelf=swoonworthy-anti-hero">swoonworthy-anti-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer316921483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7703924862354026598"><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2012/08/seduced-in-dark-by-cj-roberts-review.html'>http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a> <b>*Spoiler Free*</b><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"His touch was simple, but specific, meant to show me he could be like a lover, gentle, intimate, but also that he was a man unaccustomed to hearing the word no. Yes. I understood. He was a man, and I? I was nothing but a girl, not even a woman. I was meant to fall at his feet and worship at the altar of his masculinity, grateful that he’d deigned to acknowledge me. All this, from a simple touch."</i>
</b>- C.J. Roberts (Captive in the Dark)<br/><br/>In 20</span>
  <span id="freeText7703924862354026598" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/2012/08/seduced-in-dark-by-cj-roberts-review.html">http://samsawesomness.blogspot.com/20...</a> <b>*Spoiler Free*</b><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"His touch was simple, but specific, meant to show me he could be like a lover, gentle, intimate, but also that he was a man unaccustomed to hearing the word no. Yes. I understood. He was a man, and I? I was nothing but a girl, not even a woman. I was meant to fall at his feet and worship at the altar of his masculinity, grateful that he’d deigned to acknowledge me. All this, from a simple touch."</i>
</b>- C.J. Roberts (Captive in the Dark)<br /><br />In 2011 I ran across a book called Captive in the Dark by C.J. Roberts. I'll admit, it was cover love that first got my attention but, it seemed from the moment I read the blurb I was compelled to read this book. Even though this was not a book I would have normally read, I began my journey into The Dark Duet. Mrs. Roberts challenged me in so many ways as a reader, she took me completely out of my comfort zone, she gave me an anti-hero that I should have hated and made me love him! No matter how dark Captive in the Dark was, I continued to turn the pages. By the time I finished, I was a hot mess of emotions, and that little masochist in me wanted more of this story desperately! I fully credit Mrs. Roberts for seducing me to the dark side.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me."</i>
</b><br /><br />I had exactly three books on my "Most Wanted" list for 2012, and Seduced in the Dark was one of them. I was fortunate enough to be a beta reader for this book, and thus begins my journey into The Dark Duet #2.<br /><br />This will not be a plot review, as I don't want to spoil anything for the reader. Mrs. Roberts has an incredible literary talent that goes beyond just the words on the page. She has the ability to reach inside you and provoke a wide array of feelings and emotions. They may not always be pleasant, but for an author to be able to do what she does is incredible. This story washed trough me in waves of love, anger, pleasure, sorrow, heartbreak, and at times even humor. I can't even begin to tell you how devastatingly beautiful this book is written. I can see the growth Roberts has made as a writer, and she has a wonderful voice, keep your eye on this author she is a talent on the rise, I truly believe that!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"During the course of our time together I’d fallen in love with my captor. I’d fallen in love with his smell and his taste; his smile, kindness, and yes, even his cruelty because I knew it was a part of him."</i>
</b><br /><br />Livvy is such a strong character even in her circumstances. She's willful, stubborn and challenges Caleb on so any levels. Olivia and Caleb were scorchingly hot in this book! The dubious consent isn't as prevalent in this story. Olivia is even funny at times even when the current situation is messed up, she'll have something funny fly out of her mouth. Livvy also wears her heart on her sleeve, and there are times it's almost costly for herself and Caleb.<br /><br />Caleb.... Oh how much I adore him! I started loving him in the first book, but after this book I fell completely in love! There were a couple of times I wanted to throttle him. But some of his actions would later come back to haunt him. He's so complex, and damaged. The man that started this journey for retribution, ended up on a path of self-discovery and intense heartbreak. His story absolutely tore me up, it ripped my heart to shreds!!<br /><br />Rafiq... There has always been something unsettling to me about him. Caleb's savior, his mentor, and his teacher of sorts. It has bothered me to no end that Caleb feels he owes Rafiq unconditionally, and is constantly browbeaten with it. <br /><br />We also meet a couple of interesting new characters, Dr. Sloan and Agent Reed. It's actually the banter between these two characters and Olivia that provide some of the laughs in this story. The dynamics between Sloan and Reed could make for it's own story in the future...maybe? <br /><br />To the returning readers of this series, I can say this... You absolutely won't be disappointed. This story is one helluva ride you won't want to miss. As I approached the last quarter of the story, I felt like I stepped into a Quentin Tarantino film, it was fabulous! There were so many twists and turns to the plot, things that took me by surprise! The writing is crisp, the plot is tight, and I wasn't able to find any holes. This book is not mainstream erotica, there's a brilliant story being told, and it ended up being one of my favorite books ever!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>5 ++ Breathtakingly Brilliant Stars!!!</i>
</b> <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7703924862354026598" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_316918764" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/316918764" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/316918764?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=explicit">explicit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-bad-boy">lead-character-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=i-want-it-now">i-want-it-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=september-2012">september-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer316918764" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5972399868050478964">FIVE++ EMOTIONALLY RAW & EROTIC STARS<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Live for me, Kitten. Be all those things you’d never be with me. Go to school. Meet a normal boy and fall in love. Forget me.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>**Sob, sob, sob, sob** Oh God, just typing those words makes me cry. I fucking loved this book. I love it so much. I can’t believe it’s over. I felt nothing but hollow inside after it was done. Whatever words that I spew out for this review will never do it justice. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>Never had I wanted to laugh, and weep, and fuck, and devour an</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText5972399868050478964" style="display:none">FIVE++ EMOTIONALLY RAW &amp; EROTIC STARS<br><br><b>
  <i>“Live for me, Kitten. Be all those things you’d never be with me. Go to school. Meet a normal boy and fall in love. Forget me.”</i>
</b><br><br>**Sob, sob, sob, sob** Oh God, just typing those words makes me cry. I fucking loved this book. I love it so much. I can’t believe it’s over. I felt nothing but hollow inside after it was done. Whatever words that I spew out for this review will never do it justice. <br><br><b>
  <i>Never had I wanted to laugh, and weep, and fuck, and devour another human being until there was nothing left of him – until we were one person and I could feel peace. ~ Livvie</i>
</b><br><br>First thing I want to mention is that C.J. Roberts is one hell of a writer. The woman has got some mad skills when it comes to story telling. Holy Fuck was this story brilliantly crafted. This is one of the best books I’ve ever read. Bravo!<br><br>This was <b>
  <u>not</u>
</b> an easy read. Far from it. C.J. Roberts did not hold back the punches and I thank God, and C.J., for that. It would not have been the same if she had. This story will strip you bare, leaving you raw, traumatized and vulnerable. I literally hurt. My heart ached and my mind thoroughly fucked. This is not a pretty story. The journey is dark and filled with unimaginable things. You will not be the same when the journey is done.<br><br><b>
  <i>It seemed to Caleb, the nature of human being revolved around one empirical truth: we want what we <u>cannot</u> have. For Eve, it was the fruit of the forbidden tree. For Caleb, it was Livvie.</i>
</b><br><br>Caleb is one tortured soul. I literally cried when we find out more about his past. It is tremendously heartbreaking. He is damaged, but I don’t care. I love him. I will repeat. I love Caleb. Yes, he can be one rough son of a bitch, but underneath his cruel and tough façade, lies the true him. That despite his violent, brutal and painful past, he is just a man wanting to be accepted and loved. At least that is my theory. He seeks acceptance from Rafiq, the man who freed Caleb from his hell. He owes him everything and will do anything in his power to please him. He has remained loyal to him through everything. Ever since Livvie came into this life, he’s been rethinking this whole revenge thing, but he doesn’t want to disappoint Rafiq. And then of course, there’s Livvie. Caleb has his doubts about her. Livvie acts like she wants to run away with him; to only love him. But isn’t her ultimate goal survival? Because there is no way that a woman like Livvie would ever desire to be with a monster like him…right?<br><br><b>
  <i>My heart, independent of my logic, had reserved a place for my tormentor and my solace.</i>
</b><br><br>Even after all the mind games, the torment, the heartaches that Caleb dishes out, there is no doubt Livvie is in love with him. Her strong will is the main reason why I love her. She is one of the bravest heroines I’ve ever come across. She constantly pushes Caleb’s buttons, knowing the possible consequences because she believes wholeheartedly that he will do the right thing. Caleb constantly tests her will, trying to push her away, but she is one tough and stubborn woman. Her relationship with Caleb is complex to say the least, but Holy Mother, it is scorching. I want their relationship to work, but after all that’s happened and what’s going to happen, do they have a future?<br><br><b>
  <i>“The truth is… I wonder if I’m not fucked up, too. I should hate you, Caleb. Now I’ve decided what my fate will be. I should want to kill you. I don’t. I can’t imagine never having known you.”</i>
</b><br><br>This series has completely blown me away. Like Livvie, my emotions were everywhere. I was so conflicted. Did I enjoy my mind being fucked and toyed with? Yes. Absolutely 100%, YES. If that makes me fucked up, so be it. I’m proud of it. Because of this series, I’ve learned that my tolerance to unique tales is limitless. My mind is free and open to explore new things. I feel liberated and I feel phenomenal. Thank you, C.J. You are one amazing writer and I look forward to all of your future works.<br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>FOLLOW ME</u>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1125283864" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17047055017499497305"><br/><b>"5 <i>Mine!</i> stars"</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755438.gif' width='400' height='240' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Mine.<br/>The word was a declaration. It rocked him to his very foundation. It was a truth he’d kept hidden for far too long. Caleb didn’t know anything about love, or loving anyone, but he knew… Livvie was his.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>This is one of those times where I struggle to write a review to express my mountain size feelings in words. Until a few months back I was terrified of reading anything DARK even if it had HEA and now I can gladly say reading <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1053602034?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>“Tears of Tess”</a> is the best decision I’</span>
  <span id="freeText17047055017499497305" style="display:none"><br><b>"5 <i>Mine!</i> stars"</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380392435ra/755438.gif" width="400" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Mine.<br>The word was a declaration. It rocked him to his very foundation. It was a truth he’d kept hidden for far too long. Caleb didn’t know anything about love, or loving anyone, but he knew… Livvie was his.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote>This is one of those times where I struggle to write a review to express my mountain size feelings in words. Until a few months back I was terrified of reading anything DARK even if it had HEA and now I can gladly say reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1053602034?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">“Tears of Tess”</a> is the best decision I’ve made. There is something about the way our emotions get all tangled up while reading Dark romance, all the emotions are heightened clouding our judgement, being furious at one time and terrified the next, it’s the only time we lose the sense of thinking and pull us into whirlwind of manipulation, fear, hatred, compassion, betrayal, honesty, cruelty, desire, vengeance, passion and unconditional LOVE-that’s what <b>Seduced in the Dark</b> was for me. <br><br> I’ve said it before and I don’t mind it saying it again, Caleb and Livvie’s story is ♥EPIC♥! I know that Caleb is far from being the knight in a shining armour, I hated Caleb for better part of this story, he’s a monster in disguise who kidnapped, abused and tormented Livvie in ways nobody would wish it on their worst enemy, he’s a monster a seducer your worst nightmare but knowing him, seeing the world from his eyes and feeling his emotions will tear you apart, he has come to love and care in her company, she became his strength, his light in darkness, his salvation. Being inside Caleb mind was a torture in itself, I couldn’t fathom the situation where you have to choose between the one who saved you from the long life of misery and the one who loves you irrespective of your darkness. I finally understood why he had to do the things he did, I think I could finally forgive him, <b> “...monsters aren't born, they're made...”</b>. Yes! I love him, I’m in love with this monster. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418136898i/12680701.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Livvie <i>*sighs*</i> Words fall short to describe this epitome of forgiveness, courage, love and HOPE. Her struggle to survive and to have faith in only one person to save her is the one who happens to be her abuser. When all things are said and done she can’t hate him and can never deny the fact she’s in love with her captor. And that’s the beauty of their story they grew and transformed into different individual changing each other’s life for good and their love and passion is desirable enough to make you cuddle with your kindle and read <b>Chapter 19</b> over and over again <i>*winks*</i><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I'm yours," she said, but then added, <br>"only yours. And you're mine, only mine.”</b>
  </i>
  <b></b>
</blockquote><b>C.J Roberts is fucking genius</b> for delivering this spellbinding tale said from Livvie’s POV entwined between past and present totally capturing your undivided attention. It was dark, gritty and in so many levels disturbing yet a story so beautiful leaving you overwhelmed with emotional. Her writing is powerful and compelling that I love her for breaking my heart, fueling my rage, questioning my sense of judgement and making me fall in love with a monster. <br><br><i>Buddy read with Jasmine &amp; Kirsten♥♥<br><br>Photo courtesy: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://monal.booklikes.com/post/543624/post">http://monal.booklikes.com/post/54362...</a></i></span>

Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Seduced in the Dark</a><br /><br /><b>Dare I say PERFECT</b><br />Yes i believe I can. This book, NO this series was perfect. It was brought full circle with the ultimate betrayal in a gut-wrenching, jaw dropping heartbreaking way. And all points lead to Caleb.<br /><br /><b>Thanks for making me a fighter</b><br />Fueled by his desire to seek vengence Caleb continues forward with his plan to sell Livvie in order to kill his enemy Vladek Rostrovich. Now in route to meet with Rafiq, Caleb knows his time with Livve is limited. He has to stay on the course he started even when his heart begins to rebel against it. He knows she is just playing with him the same way he has played with her. She is smart her survival depends on him she is also strong willed and determined. He is very aware of the fact that someday <i><b>she</b> may seek revenge against him.</i><br /><br /><b>Tug of War</b><br />As revenge powered Caleb to do some unthinkable things.**Shivers** His loyalty to Rafiq seemed to only increase the onslaught of pain he inflicted on Livve most of which was done emotionally. It seemed like every time his love for her would surface he would beat it back down by taking his cruelty to another level. <br />Just when I think things couldn't get worse. They did. And Livvie.... Well, when she cried I cried. But through her tears she became the epitome of <i>resilience</i>.<br /><br /><i>Beg me...Choose me...</i><br />Every. Damn. Time he made her beg it bit him in the ass. Because soon after her love would reach out for him to <i>choose...</i><br /><br />Her love said<br /><b> Choose me<br />Want me<br />Love me<br /><i>more than revenge and over loyalty. *whispers* Choose me.</i></b><br /><br />Oh Livvie my heart broke for her a thousand times over.<br /><br /><u>Fave lines and internal monologues</u><br /><br /><i>'I'm crying again and I hate myself for it. Why won't my face stop leaking!'</i> <br />-Livvie's inner monologue<br /><br /><i>"Steady Kitten I won't let him inside you. I won't let anyone inside you."</i><br /> -Caleb<br /><br /><i>'I'm Dessert? Nice of Caleb to make me part of dinner. Bastard!</i> <br />-Livvie's inner monologue<br /><br /><i>'The naive girl in me had been bitch-slapped into womandhood. I'd been razed by pain, grief, loss and suffering, and honed by lust, rage, and an acute awareness of my need to survive.'</i> -Livvie's inner monologue<br /><br /><br /><u>Read this book!</u><br />Why should you read it? I'll tell you why! Because it is story telling at it's greatest! <br />Beautifully crafted. C.J. Roberts sculpted, shaped, carved and molded this series to perfection. It brought forth highs and lows for me. At one point I saw the PEARLY GATES and at other times i dropped to the depths of HELL. I felt like i had been sucked into a black hole from the soul churning story unfolding before my eyes. When i started the book I was in an uproar saying to myself<br />-What is going on?<br />-How did she get there?<br />-The FEDS awwwww SHIT! <br />-Where is Caleb?<br />-What the fuck happened?<br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Strong Willed and Lovable<br />Writing Style- Excellent!     </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer373383717" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3187142805735785131"><b>5 EROTICALLY DARK AND DEMENTED STARS.</b><br/><br/><br/>There are the kinds of books that come along once in awhile that leave you feeling like you've just had a mind, body and soul experience! The second book in the Dark Duet Series, Seduced in the Dark is that kind of book. As I was reading the book I felt so many intense emotions. It was brilliantly mind numbing, gripping and dark.<br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Tears ran down my face unabashed, but I didn't move to wipe them away. I had earned those tears, and I would wear them as a symb</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText3187142805735785131" style="display:none"><b>5 EROTICALLY DARK AND DEMENTED STARS.</b><br /><br /><br />There are the kinds of books that come along once in awhile that leave you feeling like you've just had a mind, body and soul experience! The second book in the Dark Duet Series, Seduced in the Dark is that kind of book. As I was reading the book I felt so many intense emotions. It was brilliantly mind numbing, gripping and dark.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Tears ran down my face unabashed, but I didn't move to wipe them away. I had earned those tears, and I would wear them as a symbol of everything I had been through. They represented all the pain I had suffered, the love I felt, and the ocean of loss sweeping through my soul. I had finally learned to obey and never looked back." ~ Livvie.</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />In this book Caleb and Livvie’s journey continues. We start out with Livvie in a hospital talking about her time with Caleb and are taken through the months of her captivity and slavery. You will go through an extremely hard and intense journey learning all that Livvie has been through and all that she has seen. The book unfolds brilliantly. There are so many facets to Caleb and the monster he is and while reading you become more aware of the depth of emotional and physical trauma he has been through, and why he’s turned into that monster! It’s really heartbreaking and I felt devastated at times for him. He’s extremely hot and cold as far as his moods towards Livvie go and that causes you to feel a wide array of emotions toward him. You go from hopeful to crazy angry to devastatingly sad in a very short amount of time. Its a pull and tug at your heart and soul, he is so gripped by revenge that Caleb can’t see anything but the vengeance he insists he needs and even though his feelings for Livvie are present he struggle’s with them because his loyalty to Rafiq runs deep. It’s truly a roller coaster ride with him and most of the time you are in a free fall state and are hanging on for your life.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I've been doing this a long time - Manipulating people to get my way. That's why you think you love me. Because I've broken you down and built you back up to believe it. It wasn't an accident. Once you leave this behind...you'll see that." ~ Caleb</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Livvie is such a beautiful character! She’s a fighter and is brave and strong. She does what she needs to; to survive after the torture and abuse she has gone through in the hands of Caleb and the other monsters in this book. She’s been sexually assaulted, beaten and emotionally abused but still manages to not let them break her down completely. While Livvie recounts her abuse you feel extremely violated and sick. It’s really hard to put into words just how damaged she is after what’s she’s been through but as she reflects on all of it, her sadness and grief are palpable...it’s hard to read. Her love and hope in Caleb is so complex and sometimes really hard to stomach. It’s a real mind f*ck at times, you struggle internally with the monster Caleb is and the way Livvie see’s him.<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"You don't know what you want, Livvie, and what you think you want, you've been brainwashed into wanting." ~ Caleb</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Honestly this is probably the best series I’ve ever read. Seduced in the dark took me on a journey that no other book has ever taken me on. It’s one of the best books I have EVER read. It’s a book that will live with me forever. It changed the way I look at life and other books, and has probably f*cked up my reading future because nothing will ever compare to the pure brilliance that this book is! CJ Roberts is amazing and I stand in Awe of her. Reading it was a full body experience. If you are looking for a crazy mind f*ck book, then you have found a treasure. This series will leave you stunned, fuzzy headed and in withdrawal for more of Caleb and Livvie.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3187142805735785131" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14033863126421345658"><b>3.75 Stars</b><br/><br/>Told in multiple POV, both in 1st & 3rd person, it’s the second installment in "The Dark duet" and has to be read in order. This was still an enjoyable read but not as much as book 1. In this one, I disliked Caleb most of the book. His confusion was exhausting and it drained me! Another thing that I hated here was Livvie’s crying! Don’t get me wrong, I was aware of her plight, believe me, but she was crying so much almost on every page her eyes were puffy and red… There was a twist tow</span>
  <span id="freeText14033863126421345658" style="display:none"><b>3.75 Stars</b><br /><br />Told in multiple POV, both in 1st &amp; 3rd person, it’s the second installment in "The Dark duet" and has to be read in order. This was still an enjoyable read but not as much as book 1. In this one, I disliked Caleb most of the book. His confusion was exhausting and it drained me! Another thing that I hated here was Livvie’s crying! Don’t get me wrong, I was aware of her plight, believe me, but she was crying so much almost on every page her eyes were puffy and red… There was a twist towards the end that I didn't see coming and it surprised me. There were interesting side characters that I'd like to know about their stories! What happened to Felipe &amp; Celia?! I’m really curious about them! And I’d like to know more about Agent Reed &amp; Dr. Sloan! Overall, despite the issues, I still had a good time reading this and hope you enjoy it as well!</span>

<div id="review_401155940" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/401155940" />
    <a title="Annie Brewer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer"><img alt="Annie Brewer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442496062p2/5315988.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/401155940?book_show_action=true">Aug 26, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie Brewer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie Brewer" href="/user/show/5315988-annie-brewer">Annie Brewer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=absolutely-amazingly-awesome">absolutely-amazingly-awesome</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=alternating-pov-s">alternating-pov-s</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=book-boyfriend">book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=favorite">favorite</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=nook-books">nook-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=hot-as-shit-fucking">hot-as-shit-fucking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=unforgettable">unforgettable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5315988-annie-brewer?shelf=5-star-worthy">5-star-worthy</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer401155940" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14601593193672418586">WOW WOW WOW I can't stop crying. This was....it was....I just. Gah, my emotions are everywhere right now. I seriously need time to process what I just read. Maybe tomorrow I can write a proper review. But holy shit. I love Caleb. LOVE him!!!! A-Fucking-Mazing!!!!!!<br/><br/><br/>“Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.” <br/><br/>Well, I just realized I never did my review for Captive in the Dark. So I will have to rectify the situation-what an absurd ordeal. Though out of the t</span>
  <span id="freeText14601593193672418586" style="display:none">WOW WOW WOW I can't stop crying. This was....it was....I just. Gah, my emotions are everywhere right now. I seriously need time to process what I just read. Maybe tomorrow I can write a proper review. But holy shit. I love Caleb. LOVE him!!!! A-Fucking-Mazing!!!!!!<br /><br /><br />“Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.” <br /><br />Well, I just realized I never did my review for Captive in the Dark. So I will have to rectify the situation-what an absurd ordeal. Though out of the two, I would have to say this book is my favorite. And yes, it's MUCH more intense, darker, more hair pulling, eye gauging, wanna slap a bitch up fucked up book and I wouldn't have it any other way!!!! I seriously wanted to scream, punch holes in the wall, throw my laptop and phone down on the ground in surrender and ram my car into a tree. That is how disturbing and dark this book is. My thoughts became so volatile and wretched, I had to force myself to stop reading sometimes. It consumed me-my every thought. I was a wreck. I couldn't sleep well and I didn't eat much while reading this for fear of retching. Some parts were so appalling I didn't know why I was reading it. I kept saying, "What the fuck am I still enamored by this damn book? It's making me sick."<br /><br />But then my answer, the only answer it could be....CALEB. CALEB. CALEB. CALEB. CALEB.<br />Yeah, I was in love with Caleb. I'm guilty! <br /><br />“So, that's it? You think I'm just some idiot that fell for your bullshit! Well you're wrong! I fell in love with you, Caleb. I fell in love with your sick sense of humor. I fell in love with the way you protected me. You saved my life!" - Livvie” <br /><br />Ahhh, didn't he save us all??? God, how I love him! He's mine Livvie!<br /><br />"Mine!"<br /><br />I knew this book would be an emotional rollercoaster as was Captive in the Dark. But daaaaaaamn, I hadn't anticipated all the sharp turns and hills, going up and down, side to side then plummeting to my death. Woaaaaah, let's put on the breaks please. This ride was a lot of things. All the things we discover about these characters made me say "WHAT????" But through most of it, I just sat there numb and cried. <br /><br />Livvie. Oh how I loved this stupid awesome girl. We both had something in common in falling for the psycho sicko. She was such a stronger more fearless girl in this book. Everything she went through made her so brave. You felt her pain, literally. You wanted to hold her while she cried and tell her it would be okay-or just take her and run the fuck out of there. You wanted to protect her and keep her safe from those sick fucks! You just wanted to be there to support her. I admire Olivia's character very much. Oh my gosh, the pain, agony, despair she suffered through most of it was enough to send you to the mental house. I really loved her. I found myself though, wishing I was in her place. (Yes, I'm a total whack job, I know.) But it's true. I'll take her place. <br />You hear that Caleb??? Pick ME ME ME!!!!! I'll be your prisoner!<br /><br /><br />Livvie Quotes:<br /><br />“I love you, Caleb. I love you! If you care for me at all... please, don't do this! Please, don't leave me. I don't know how to live without you. Don't make me go back to trying to be someone I don't know how to be anymore. - Livvie” <br /><br />“Softly, he inhales and exhales as we kiss. He never stops kissing me; he simply continues to steal my breath, returning it to me only when he’s infused it with his essence. Pure lust lives inside him. Every breath I take should come from his lungs.”<br /><br />“In the dark, my master let down his guard and he was Caleb again. He didn’t correct me. He didn’t punish me. He didn’t push me away emotionally. Caleb was there to hold me until the nightmares passed. He was there to tell me I was beautiful. He was there to tell me I was going to be okay. In the dark, he seduced me. I didn’t want the seduction to end.” <br /><br />“I'm fucked in the head, too. Even before I met you.” <br /><br />“I don’t want revenge, Caleb. I don’t want to end up like you, letting some fucking vendetta run my life. I just want my freedom. I want to be free, Caleb. Not someone’s whore…not even yours.” <br /><br />“The naïve girl in me had been bitch-slapped into womanhood. I’d been razed by pain, grief, loss and suffering, and honed by lust, rage and an acute awareness of my need to survive.” <br /><br /><br />Caleb. Oh my, what to really say about Caleb?? I loved him in Captive. Though he was fucked up in that one too-but worse in this book. I came to love him more. In Seduced, we really see another side to him that we're not used to. It's a wonderful side but still very unfamiliar. One minute he shows a smidge of kindness then the next he's whipping her like a dog. It was disturbing yet I couldn't stop reading. I wanted to hate him and a part of me did, but when I got glimpses of the Caleb that could love another person or the Caleb that felt remorse for the things he'd done-or even the Caleb that would let himself feel...something other than the lust for revenge, I knew that deep within his rage and anger, he was just one fucked up lost soul that needed to be saved. THAT Caleb I loved with all my heart because once he knew that it was okay to be human and make mistakes, he was everything Livvie needed-and me too. Ha! Honestly, as effed up as loving him sounds, I would be stupid not to. He was mislead, betrayed, lied to, raped, beaten to a bloody pulp, deceived and transformed into a monster. But it wasn't his fault. Yes, he did bad, very bad unspeakable things. Very disturbing and unforgiveable things. And I guess there are no excuses for that. BUT because of his fucked up childhood, he didn't know any better. Maybe he did as an adult, but he was already in so deep, how can one recover from that? My heart broke for him. I cried for him. I felt his pain, anguish, longing, loneliness, betrayal, hatred...I felt all of that too! It was horrible!!! My poor Caleb!! Oh how I would fix you poor, tortured boy!<br /><br />Caleb Quotes:<br /><br /> “I've been doing this a long time- manipulating people to get my way. That's why you think you love me. Because I've broken you down and built you back up to believe it. It wasn't an accident. Once you leave this behind..... you'll see that. -Caleb” <br /><br />“That you could fix me? What's more, that I could fix you? Well, Sorry, pet, I don't want to be fixed. - Caleb”<br /><br />“Mine.<br />The word was a declaration. It rocked him to his very foundation. It was a truth he’d kept hidden for far too long. Caleb didn’t know anything about love, or loving anyone, but he knew… Livvie was his.” <br /><br />“She kisses my scars and I create new ones for her.”<br /><br />“What are you doing ?" She said and laughed. <br />"I was curious," he whispered. <br />"About what ?"<br />"If happy tears taste the same as the sad ones," he said.”<br /><br />“Live for me, Kitten. Be all those things you'd never be with me. Go to school. Meet a normal boy and fall in love. Forgive me. It's time for you to go, Kitten. Time for us both, to go.” <br /><br /><br />All in al, this book was definitely a tossing-turning kind of ride. I recommend these books to those that can handle the Fifty Shades books. Though these are darker and more fucked up, I say they are BETTER!!! If you love Fifty-you'll love Caleb MORE!!! Seriously, these were incredible. What a joy ride! But be prepared for the shock and clusterfuck of shit that happens! You'll be mentally and emotionally drained by the end. God, one minute I was screaming in rage-the next I was weeping for Caleb-then sobbing for Livvie and all she had to endure-then I was in shock-turned disgust-to hatred filled madness. Oh what a bloody mess! The end. Oh God, I can't say much but I will say the last 35% of this book had me on pins and needles. I couldn't sit still. I couldn't be disturbed. I ignored my kids to find out what happened to our beloved Olivia and Caleb. All I will say is.....<br /><br />READ IT!!!! You won't regret it-maybe but if so...then that is your fault. I am saying now, it's dark and so effed up. But it is worth every bit!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14601593193672418586" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer330358853" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12771048997873187112"><b>WOW! Just WOW! PRAISE THE ALMIGHTY CJ ROBERTS. BOW DOWN TO HER!!!</b> ;)<br/><br/>Never in my life have I felt so consumed in a story.  I felt it all.  The guilt, the jealousy, the sorrow, and at the end of it all I felt the desperation and need to run away from it.    <br/><br/>Ms. Roberts has an amazing way of weaving a story to keep the reader guessing at which way the story will go.  There are so many twists and turns that you almost get whiplash from the force of the revelations.  And boy are there some doozies!!!</span>
  <span id="freeText12771048997873187112" style="display:none"><b>WOW! Just WOW! PRAISE THE ALMIGHTY CJ ROBERTS. BOW DOWN TO HER!!!</b> ;)<br /><br />Never in my life have I felt so consumed in a story.  I felt it all.  The guilt, the jealousy, the sorrow, and at the end of it all I felt the desperation and need to run away from it.    <br /><br />Ms. Roberts has an amazing way of weaving a story to keep the reader guessing at which way the story will go.  There are so many twists and turns that you almost get whiplash from the force of the revelations.  And boy are there some doozies!!!  There were moments I had to do a double take at what I had just read.   <br />Don’t miss out, get this book Sept 1, 2012.  From the first word to the last, you wont be disappointed!!!<br /><br />Okay, I’m not gonna lie, I was kinda upset cuz the beginning of the story was just like a book I’d already read so the epicness of my anticipation for the book went down a peg.  It was the same set up, went from present to past with the police questioning the victim.  Now that’s where the similarities ended and where the story took off.  It had me holding my breath as I eagerly waited for the next blow.   <br /><br />Livvi was a victim in Captive in the Dark.  Not in this one.  Yes there are moments where Caleb treats her as his slave but behind closed doors something has blossomed into unfamiliar territory, for both of them.  <br /><br />Livvi never felt love from anyone, not even from her own mother and Caleb oh my poor poor Caleb.  Taken at such a young age he doesn’t know any better.  <br /><br />Felipe, an associate of Rafiq’s, has housed Caleb and Livvi aka Kitten so he can train her to be a proper slave for the unsuspecting Vladek.  As their pawn, Kitten is to be Vladek’s for 2 years.  During this training Caleb feels things he’s never felt and is falling for Kitten.  Unbeknownst to both Caleb and Kitten, Felipe has watched their relationship unfold and is willing to use it against them to gain better footing with Rafiq’s role in his own life.  <br /><br />To prove to Felipe and mainly to himself that he isn’t falling for Kitten he has her attend a party where she would be used as entertainment for all to see and enjoy.  A side of him he’s never seen comes to light, jealous, hot and biting consumes him.  He whisks her away and takes all his anger and lust out of her.  From there on Kitten’s virginity can no longer be used as a bargaining tool.  Caleb takes what is his and wont let go of Kitten.  Deep down he knows that Rafiq will not like the turn of events but he is hopeful that things will work out in his favor.<br /><br />Rafiq, what a sick and twisted man.  He’s not the man Caleb thought he was.  He more evil and very calculating in his game.  He will stop at nothing to get his revenge.  In the end the student exceeds his teacher.<br /><br />Present: Agent Reed has been questioning Livvi for days and at first she reveals nothing.  She only wants the one man she’s ever loved, Caleb.  Slowly with the assistance of Dr. Sloan agent Reed is able to get Livvi’s story.  Its full of tragic loss and Reed cant help but relate.  Everyone has a past that’s unforgettable.  <br /><br />I am so happy to say with all the shit that went down there is a HEA!  I promise!  Don’t give up on hope, keep reading.  There is light at the end of the of the dark tunnel!<br /><br />for this review along with my others please visit my blog<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.upallnightreviews.blogspot.com">www.upallnightreviews.blogspot.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12771048997873187112" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_3574269650" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3574269650" />
    <a title="Ida" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23173697-ida"><img alt="Ida" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1423853357p2/23173697.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3574269650?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ida" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ida" href="/user/show/23173697-ida">Ida</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3574269650" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10884293487951618556"><blockquote>
  <i>Monsters aren’t born – they’re made.</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602150265ra/30208130.gif' width='' height='' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This is <b>not</b> romance.<br/>This is <b>not</b> BDSM. <br/><blockquote>
  <i>"BDSM is a <b>consensual, agreed</b> and often erotic interaction that involves elements of bondage and discipline, dominance and submission, or sadism and masochism."</i>
</blockquote><br/>The book is dark and it's erotic, yes, but for something to be labeled romance I feel the "relationship" has to be consensual. It's still very gritty and most of the book is on the verge of uncomfortable, but the storyline and characters kept me interested t</span>
  <span id="freeText10884293487951618556" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>Monsters aren’t born – they’re made.</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602150265ra/30208130.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is <b>not</b> romance.<br>This is <b>not</b> BDSM. <br><blockquote>
  <i>"BDSM is a <b>consensual, agreed</b> and often erotic interaction that involves elements of bondage and discipline, dominance and submission, or sadism and masochism."</i>
</blockquote><br>The book is dark and it's erotic, yes, but for something to be labeled romance I feel the "relationship" has to be consensual. It's still very gritty and most of the book is on the verge of uncomfortable, but the storyline and characters kept me interested throughout the book. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>It seemed to Caleb that the nature of human beings revolved around one empirical truth: we want what we cannot have. For Eve, it was the fruit of the forbidden tree. For Caleb, it was Livvie.</i>
</blockquote><br>Most of us read fantasy and fiction so we can go on adventures we otherwise would never get to experience, and this book definitely let's you "experience" something I hope I'll never ever get even close to experiencing in real life. <br><br>I still enjoyed the authors writing, but I got a little hung up on some of the repetitive wording, like <br><blockquote>
  <i>"My heart is beating a frantic tattoo"<br>"My heart pounded a sharp tattoo"<br>"His heart beat a frantic tattoo"<br>"His heart pounded a sharp tattoo"</i>
</blockquote><br>*Sort of spoilers below this point* <br><br>Before starting this book I read some spoiler free reviews to prepare myself, because I thought this book would be much much worse than the first, but after having built up suspense for half the book I can honestly say the breaking point was a big let down. It's probably because I still don't like Caleb, and therefore I felt no emotions when reading from his POV.. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602150265ra/30208131.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I still like Livvie and feel her character is portrayed really well. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>For the love of Christ, shut – up! Let a bitch enjoy her mental breakdown in peace.</i>
</blockquote><br>I do feel ready to part with this story and its characters, but how often do you get a 200 paged epilogue? Imma buy the third book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602150265ra/30208132.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Be smart! Fight the battles you can win and accept the ones you can’t. That’s how you survive.”</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="10884293487951618556" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385595i/744592._SY540_.png' width='350' height='450' alt='kiss' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>This book is DARK and very captivating, crazy good, deep and it will probably make your therapist rich!</b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“He had told her he wasn't her Prince Charming, but what he hadn't said, was he wished he could be</b>
</i><br/><br/>Yupp, Thats <b>Caleb!</b> A dark knight... A zombie with a heart beat, A monster just like 'Beast' from Beauty and the Beast. <b>A monster with a heart of gold.</b><br/><br/><i>We want what we cannot have. For Eve, it was the fruit of </i></span>
  <span id="freeText7303644037671339578" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“Once upon a time, Caleb held me captive in the dark, now he used it to seduce me.”</b>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385595i/744592._SY540_.png" width="350" height="450" alt="kiss" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>This book is DARK and very captivating, crazy good, deep and it will probably make your therapist rich!</b><br><br><i>
  <b>“He had told her he wasn't her Prince Charming, but what he hadn't said, was he wished he could be</b>
</i><br><br>Yupp, Thats <b>Caleb!</b> A dark knight... A zombie with a heart beat, A monster just like 'Beast' from Beauty and the Beast. <b>A monster with a heart of gold.</b><br><br><i>We want what we cannot have. For Eve, it was the fruit of the forbidden tree. For Caleb, it was Livvie.</i><br><br><b>Livvie..</b> Sweet strong girl! I really want to give her a round of applause and a bow, along with the author!<br>Kitten is so strong, beautiful and amazing smart!! She fought till the end and got what she wanted the most.<br><i>       <b>‘If it be thus to dream, still let me sleep’</b><br>                      – William Shakespeare</i><br><br><br>I feel so giggy happy and so glad that I read this book at last! I admit I was shit scared but then I just had to because, hell.. dark works for me!<br>So where do I start this review?<br><br>Let me say, <b>I LOVED THIS BOOK!</b> Probabily more than the first book if not the same amount! It was <b>Insane Mindfuckingly Good.</b> I felt like I read 'Inception' or something! :P<br>If that book left you in a daze, god help you with this one!<br><br>This book was impeccably good, the story, the whole plot, the way its written and brought up and in a way the author's shed light on something so important that we turn a blind eye too! About slavery, human trafficking, about the illegal things rich powerful people do! How innocents suffer each and everyday! Gosh! x_x<br><br>This book unravels so much! So many twists and turns and bumps along the way! So much gets enfolded! We learn so much about Caleb's past, about things which lead to him being where he is today.<br>The book hurts, its like a punch in the gut! Its sad, it makes you feel too much! Anger, pain, sorrow, pity and so much more!! It makes you want to kill.<br><br>I really liked the book, I loved all the side characters and I am glad they will be getting a spinoff!<br><b>Agent Reed!!</b> Hell, his book is going to be something!!<br><pre>Thoughts as I proceeded during this book..</pre><br><b>
  <i>[5% into the book]</i>
</b><br>I wanted to tear it, and probably stom on it, but yes.. I kept yelling 'ITS A LIE, ITS A LIE' at it like a wack job!<br><br><b>
  <i>[15-20%]</i>
</b><br>My brain hurts!! This is effing brilliant!<br><br><b>
  <i>[30% onwards]</i>

<div id="review_318520889" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/318520889" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/318520889?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer318520889" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8108651002478075904">**DOES NOT CONTAIN SPOILERS**<br/><br/>Check out our blog for our video interview with CJ Roberts: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/2012/08/21/interview-with-cj-roberts-and-totallybookedblog-21st-august-2012/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/2012/08/...</a><br/><br/>This was definitely one of the most gut-wrenchingly difficult, raw, brutal, thought provoking and emotional reads I have ever sat through. There were times I thought I couldn’t go on and my resolve was sorely tested<br/><br/>My chest ached, my stomach was in knots and more than once I felt physically sick with the anticipation of what was about to happen.<br/><br/>Reading this book I felt</span>
  <span id="freeText8108651002478075904" style="display:none">**DOES NOT CONTAIN SPOILERS**<br /><br />Check out our blog for our video interview with CJ Roberts: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2012/08/21/interview-with-cj-roberts-and-totallybookedblog-21st-august-2012/">http://totallybookedblog.com/2012/08/...</a><br /><br />This was definitely one of the most gut-wrenchingly difficult, raw, brutal, thought provoking and emotional reads I have ever sat through. There were times I thought I couldn’t go on and my resolve was sorely tested<br /><br />My chest ached, my stomach was in knots and more than once I felt physically sick with the anticipation of what was about to happen.<br /><br />Reading this book I felt that CJ must be one of the most talented writers I’ve ever read. How she crafted this story and brought it all together left me in total awe. She is a storyteller who certainly doesn’t shy away from what she feels needs to be told, even if, at times, this makes the reader uncomfortable and takes them to a place they thought they could never go.<br /><br />The reader is taken from the time Livvie is captured and from there she recounts how her predicament evolved and how Caleb and the others played a part in her story. It was nothing short of brilliant how this story was pieced together.<br /><br />Caleb is still the broken “monster” we met in Captive in the Dark. He is hell-bent on his revenge and willing to sacrifice Livvie (Kitten) into slavery just to ensure his task is carried out.<br /><br />I have to admit to having strong feelings for Caleb when reading Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet #1). I hated him because I loved him, when really I should have despised him. Nothing changes in this book. I was still questioning my sanity over my feelings for this man. How could I, after what he had done and was still prepared to do, feel so much love and compassion for him? What was it about this man that drew me to him? Oh trust me, there were times when I wanted to knife him through the heart. This man will test you, and he will test you BIG time, but his tender times with Livvie will hit you deep in your heart and it is at these times when you feel, when you hope, that there is goodness and perhaps love somewhere in this man.<br /><br />Livvie has grown in this book. She has feelings for Caleb that have her questioning if she is of sound mind. How could she feel the way she does for Caleb after what he has done to her? After what he was still intending to do to her? He never sugar coated her fate. You will be clenching your heart for Livvie. You can’t put yourself in her shoes because you couldn’t withstand the heartbreak of being there.<br /><br />I will tell you now that I cried reading this book more than I have ever cried reading a book before. Whilst this story is at times shocking, it was also so emotional throughout, and catching glimpses of Caleb’s past will have you clutching your chest. I defy anyone to read the last chapter of this book without crying.<br /><br />After finishing this book I sobbed for an hour afterwards and just stared into space. I had to absorb everything I had read and marvel at what an amazing and emotional journey this author had just taken me on.<br /><br />As I’ve said, this is by no means an easy read, let’s face it, a book about human trafficking and sex slavery was never written with the intention of being an easy read.<br /><br />However, when you pick this book up (be sure to read Captive in the Dark first!) you will experience, what I can promise you will be an emotional rollercoaster the likes of which you will be hard pressed to beat.<br /><br />This book will make you angry. It will make you sick. It will make you sad. It will test your resolve. It will make you question your thoughts and your feelings, but I promise you, you will not forget this book. It will stay with you long after the last page, because not only will this book touch your heart, it will touch your soul.<br /><br /><b>Side note:<b><br /><br />Whilst reading this book I was listening Jack White’s new album and the lyrics to Love Interruption reminded me of Caleb so much it sort of became my theme song for this book.<br /><br />I was blown away when one of my fellow Beta readers Rhonda had chosen the same song, and posted it on her FB page, so I wanted to share it with you here.<br /><br />So….Rhonda, Yajaira (our other Beta reader) &amp; CJ – this one’s for you girls and our beautiful Caleb (oh, and Paul Walker xo) xxxx <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iErNRBTPbEc">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=iErNRB...</a><br /><br /><br /><br /><br />(Please note: I was a Beta reader for this book)<br /><br /> </b></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8108651002478075904" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Mona" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6013607-mona"><img alt="Mona" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565358189p2/6013607.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/646421079?book_show_action=true">Jun 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mona" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mona" href="/user/show/6013607-mona">Mona</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Dark Read Lovers!</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6013607-mona?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer646421079" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4049710733218316493"><i>
  <b>"You could not sell me...I could stay with you...be with you?"</b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426109i/851056._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='580' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>Vivisected. On-off-buzz-buzz-on-off. Caleb I miss you.</b>
</i> <br/> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380739163ra/3117565.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I didn't expect this story to begin the way it did. Maybe if I had known, I wouldn't have hesitated for so long before starting this. I expected to start where I left off in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_' title='Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts' rel='nofollow noopener'>Captive in the Dark</a>, scared of Rafiq's arrival, but to my surprise I was pushed into the present and all my questions on how Livvie and Caleb's story unfolded were left in the past, to be revealed lat</span>
  <span id="freeText4049710733218316493" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"You could not sell me...I could stay with you...be with you?"</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426109i/851056._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="580" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>Vivisected. On-off-buzz-buzz-on-off. Caleb I miss you.</b>
</i> <br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380739163ra/3117565.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I didn't expect this story to begin the way it did. Maybe if I had known, I wouldn't have hesitated for so long before starting this. I expected to start where I left off in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12513614.Captive_in_the_Dark__The_Dark_Duet___1_" title="Captive in the Dark (The Dark Duet, #1) by C.J. Roberts" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive in the Dark</a>, scared of Rafiq's arrival, but to my surprise I was pushed into the present and all my questions on how Livvie and Caleb's story unfolded were left in the past, to be revealed later on in the book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380739163ra/3117566.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I got a clear insight on Livvie's thoughts and feeling for Caleb through this book. I truly felt as though I was there as she retell the story from her perspective. I understood how someone can fall in love with a person like Caleb. Her kidnapper and abuser. Someone with the intentions of selling her for revenge. I felt her love, sorrow and need for Caleb.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426109i/851057._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Its amazing how talented this author is. I was captivated to the point of believing I was apart of this story. I could feel their pain, as though it was mine. My heart ached for the circumstances they were in. For their impossible love. I felt anxiety, my heart racing in fear for their fate at the hands of sick monster like Rafiq. And then came their love, although dark and raw, took my breath away. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426109i/851059._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There were times throughout this book were, I'll admit, I hated Caleb. Even when I understood his reasons and motives for treating Livvie the way he did, I still couldn't stop from cringing and wishing he would change. And then I would understand how Livvie felt. To love someone even when you hate them. That's what Caleb does. He makes you dependent on him, craving him however you can get him, wanting him happy and loving him no matter what.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380739163i/3117567._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My heart broke for this beautiful, yet damaged man. Some of his faults, though unforgivable, can be forgotten when looking at Caleb as a whole. From his devastating past, to the betrayals he learns about, from the people who led him to become the man, looked on as a monster. He thought himself undeserving of happiness, when in truth he deserved it most. For me, Caleb couldn't have been more perfect. I loved how vulnerable he became when doubting Livvie's feelings for him and the hardship he went through when making choices against his better beliefs.<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i><b>Livvie was his. He owned her. He possessed her and he knew, with everything he was, he couldn't give her away.<br><br>Mine!</b></i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380739163i/3117568.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426109i/851058._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="340" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seduced in the dark literally blew my mind away. Even though I started off thinking I might not like this...I can say, with all my heart, that I couldn't have asked for a better story. Its beautiful but dark, raw and intense. Its filled with love, but no rainbows and sunshine. You'll be sucked into a world where Masters with slaves are the norm and punishment is a pleasure for the disobedient.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1335114363l/13612739.jpg" width="400" height="540" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>A very tragic love story, but a love story all the same.</b>
</i> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
